	--References
	idTaissaFollower = Hydra.QuestGetFollower(S_TAISSA_FOLLOWER)	
	idDonanFollower = Hydra.QuestGetFollower(S_DONAN_FOLLOWER)	
	
	idDonanSwamp = Hydra.ActorsInGroup("QST_Hawe_Verge6_Donan_Swamp_NPC")[1]
	idTaissaSwamp = Hydra.ActorsInGroup("QST_Hawe_Verge6_Taissa_Swamp_NPC")[1]
	idBrew = Hydra.ActorsInGroup("QST_Hawe_Verge5_WitchBrew")[1]

	LOC_DONAN_01 = Hydra.ActorsInGroup("QST_Hawe_Verge6_Donan_Swamp_Loc_01")[1]
	LOC_DONAN_02 = Hydra.ActorsInGroup("QST_Hawe_Verge6_Donan_Swamp_Loc_02")[1]
	LOC_TAISSA_00 = Hydra.ActorsInGroup("QST_Hawe_Verge6_Taissa_Swamp_Loc_00")[1]
	LOC_TAISSA_01 = Hydra.ActorsInGroup("QST_Hawe_Verge6_Taissa_Swamp_Loc_01")[1]

	--Donan + Taissa Move to Static
	if Hydra.ActorIsValid(idDonanFollower) then
		Hydra.QuestFollowerTakeOwnership(idDonanFollower)
		Hydra.QActorEnableAI(idDonanFollower, false)
		Hydra.QActorPlaySimpleConversation(CONVO_DONAN_01, idDonanFollower)
		Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(idDonanFollower, idDonanSwamp, "NPC_RUN", true)
		Hydra.QActorFaceSameAsActor(idDonanFollower, idDonanSwamp)
	end
	
	if Hydra.ActorIsValid(idTaissaFollower) then
		Hydra.QuestFollowerTakeOwnership(idTaissaFollower)
		Hydra.QActorEnableAI(idTaissaFollower, false)
		Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(idTaissaFollower, idTaissaSwamp, "NPC_RUN", true)
		Hydra.QActorFaceSameAsActor(idTaissaFollower, idTaissaSwamp)
		Hydra.QActorSetAnimSetOverride(idTaissaFollower, ANIMSET_TAISSA_CROUCH)
	end	
	
	Hydra.WaitForQEmpty(idTaissaFollower)
	Hydra.QActorFadeAndDelete(idDonanFollower, 0.5)
	Hydra.WaitForQEmpty(idDonanFollower)
	Hydra.QActorFadeAndDelete(idTaissaFollower, 0.5)
